Logic - 

It checks if the input XML contains a specific structure with the following elements:

s3:E2EDL20003GRP
s3:E2TXTH8001GRP
s3:E2TXTH8001 with a child element s3:TDID containing the text value 'Y030'.

If this structure is found in the input XML, the XSLT logic does the following:

It creates a new <REF> element in the output XML.
Inside the <REF> element, it creates a <REF01> element with the value 'CO'.
It extracts a specific piece of text content from the input XML (s3:E2TXTP8/s3:TDLINE) and assigns it to the $varCOTdLine variable.
It assigns the value 'CustRef:CO:' to the $findco variable.
It creates a <REF02> element and calculates its value by taking the portion of text in $varCOTdLine that appears after 'CustRef:CO:'.

Failed Case 

0083463857  - Indian Oxygen ASN

<E2TXTP8>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>E2TXTP8</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>450</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>0000000023011176</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>000023</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>000022</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>04</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>
					<TDFORMAT>*</TDFORMAT>
					<TDLINE>UPS GROUND 437933</TDLINE> CustRef:CO:516563
					<SEGMENTPAD/>
				</E2TXTP8>

Success Case - 
0083435160  - IndianOxygen ASN

<E2TXTP8>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>E2TXTP8</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>450</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>0000000022881564</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>000023</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>
					<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>000022</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>

1)The HL segment defines a top-down/left-right ordered structure.
2)HL01 shall contain a unique alphanumeric number for each occurrence of the HL segment in the transaction
set. For example, HL01 could be used to indicate the number of occurrences of the HL segment, in which
case the value of HL01 would be "1" for the initial HL segment and would be incremented by one in each
subsequent HL segment within the transaction.
3)HL02 identifies the hierarchical ID number of the HL segment to which the current HL segment is subordinate.

1)The HL segment defines a top-down/left-right ordered structure.
2)HL01 shall contain a unique alphanumeric number for each occurrence of the HL segment in the transaction
set. For example, HL01 could be used to indicate the number of occurrences of the HL segment, in which
case the value of HL01 would be "1" for the initial HL segment and would be incremented by one in each
subsequent HL segment within the transaction.
3)HL02 identifies the hierarchical ID number of the HL segment to which the current HL segment is subordinate.

P3:INC9017851:MSC Invoice failure due to missing ShipDate - Invoice #0093257860 & #0093257876  - biztalk 


Action :

1)Based on the invoices #0093257860 & #0093257876 kindly search the respective IDOC.
2)Search for the below mention field <E2EDK03 block with <IDDAT>026</IDDAT> , copy it and past it immidiatly after ending of this filed </E2EDK03>
  
<E2EDK03 xmlns="http://Microsoft.LobServices.Sap/2007/03/Types/Idoc/3/INVOIC02//701">
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>E2EDK03</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>450</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>0000000022881366</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>000012</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>000000</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>02</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>
			<IDDAT>026</IDDAT>
			<DATUM>20230919</DATUM>
			<UZEIT/>
			<SEGMENTPAD/>
		</E2EDK03>

3)Once you paste it change the IDDAT from <IDDAT>026</IDDAT> to <IDDAT>001</IDDAT> and save it.

<E2EDK03 xmlns="http://Microsoft.LobServices.Sap/2007/03/Types/Idoc/3/INVOIC02//701">
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>E2EDK03</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>450</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>0000000022881366</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>000012</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>000000</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>02</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>
			<IDDAT>001</IDDAT>
			<DATUM>20230919</DATUM>
			<UZEIT/>
			<SEGMENTPAD/>
		</E2EDK03>

4)Copy it and reprocess this IDOC file to respective location.
5)Go to 810 folder in the Outbound and verify the EDI file.
6)In the EDI file you will notice the correct date in the filed of DTM
 
Resolution - MSC invoice idoc is reprocessed by adding E2EDK03 block with IDDAT = 001

P4:INC9025635:Robertsoxygen POACK failure due to "Leading or trailing space found" & "Mandatory data element missing ACK01". POACK #864253 & #864237 - biztalk
P4:INC9025636:Robertsoxygen POACK failure due to Mandatory data element missing ACK01. POACK ##864237 - SAP 


864253 - This needs to be correct and reporcessed from biztalk end.

An unexpected failure occurred when processing a message. The text associated with the exception is "Error: 1 (Field level error)
	SegmentID: PID
	Position in TS: 9
	Data Element ID: PID05
	Position in Segment: 5
	Data Value: 
	6: Leading or trailing space found". 

When we reprocess the the failed document from biztalk end then we have to follow below steps.

1) Rober Oxygen - Invalid character :
- find out BSN no from Console
- Save the failed message localay from console
- Search all PID05 and find out where exactly invalid character is mention. mostly you will get *** as invalid character. Note down the data for which invalid character ocured for PID05.
- Find the IDOC file from respective folder with BSN no and powershell script. follow the same steps to find the the IDOC file using powershell script.
- OPent the IDOC file and search for the invalid character. here in IDOC you will not get the filed by name PID05 so you can search the *** AND data. (data you already find out from the console saved file)
- dont format IDOC file into the readable format , just open it and remove the invalid character (*** ) and save the file to local folder.
- Reprocess this IDOC file from respecive folder i.e. AllTransaction foder.
- Continue monitoring biztalk running messsges and failed messages and make sure the manual reprocess files has been processed by biztalk.
- close the open respecive ticket. 

2) Rober Oxygen - Leading or trailing space found

- find out BSN no from Console
- Save the failed message localay from console
- Search all PID05 and find out where exactly "Leading or trailing space found" is mention. Note down the data for which "Leading or trailing space found" ocured for PID05.
- Find the IDOC file from respective folder with BSN no and powershell script. follow the same steps to find the the IDOC file using powershell script.
- OPent the IDOC file and search for the invalid character. here in IDOC you will not get the filed by name PID05 so you can search the data. (data you already find out from the console saved file)
- dont format IDOC file into the readable format , just open it and remove the "Leading or trailing space found" and save the file to local folder.
- Reprocess this IDOC file from respecive folder i.e. AllTransaction foder.
- Continue monitoring biztalk running messsges and failed messages and make sure the manual reprocess files has been processed by biztalk.
- close the open respecive ticket.

P3:INC9028136:MSC Invoice failure due to missing ShipDate - Invoice #0093283809   - biztalk 

Action Steps :

1)Based on the invoices #0093283809 kindly search the respective IDOC.
2)Search for the below mention field <E2EDK03 block with <IDDAT>026</IDDAT> , copy it and past it immidiatly after ending of this filed </E2EDK03>
  
Eg. 

<E2EDK03 xmlns="http://Microsoft.LobServices.Sap/2007/03/Types/Idoc/3/INVOIC02//701">
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>E2EDK03</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>450</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>0000000022881366</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>000012</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>000000</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>02</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>
			<IDDAT>026</IDDAT>
			<DATUM>20230919</DATUM>
			<UZEIT/>
			<SEGMENTPAD/>
		</E2EDK03>

Above IDOC block is for reference only and it does not point mention #0093283809.
 
3)Once you paste it change the IDDAT from <IDDAT>026</IDDAT> to <IDDAT>001</IDDAT> and save it.

<E2EDK03 xmlns="http://Microsoft.LobServices.Sap/2007/03/Types/Idoc/3/INVOIC02//701">
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>E2EDK03</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNAM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>450</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_MANDT>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>0000000022881366</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_DOCNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>000012</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_SEGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>000000</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_PSGNUM>
			<DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>02</DATAHEADERCOLUMN_HLEVEL>
			<IDDAT>001</IDDAT>
			<DATUM>20230919</DATUM>
			<UZEIT/>
			<SEGMENTPAD/>
		</E2EDK03>

4)Copy it and reprocess this IDOC file to respective location.
5)Go to 810 folder in the Outbound and verify the EDI file.
6)In the EDI file you will notice the correct date in the filed of DTM
 
Resolution - MSC invoice idoc is reprocessed by adding E2EDK03 block with IDDAT = 001

number.

1)The HL segment defines a top-down/left-right ordered structure.
2)HL01 shall contain a unique alphanumeric number for each occurrence of the HL segment in the transaction
set. For example, HL01 could be used to indicate the number of occurrences of the HL segment, in which
case the value of HL01 would be "1" for the initial HL segment and would be incremented by one in each
subsequent HL segment within the transaction.
3)HL02 identifies the hierarchical ID number of the HL segment to which the current HL segment is subordinate.
